   <script>
    $(function() {
 $('#gnf_header, #gnf_footer').find('a').each(function(idx) {
   var el = $(this), href = el.attr('href');
   if (!!href &amp;&amp; href.startsWith('{')) {
     href = href.replace('{profile}', shc.URLs.profile)
                .replace('{orderCenter}', shc.URLs.orderCenter)
                .replace('{searsCard}', shc.URLs.searsCard)
                .replace('{listCenter}', shc.URLs.listCenter);

     el.attr('href', href);
   }
 });

 if (!!$.cookie('irp-preview')){
  FED.Util.addJsFile(shc.URLs.staticAssets + 'js/previewHeader');
 }
});
   </script>

  <script>
   $(document).on(shcWidgets.EVENTS.gnfLoaded, function() {
	var oasPositionRight = true,
		_mainContent,
		_oasContainer,
		oasLegacySpacing = function () {
			var winWidth = $(window).width();
			if (oasPositionRight &amp;&amp; winWidth &lt;= 1200) {
				_oasContainer
					.insertBefore(_mainContent)
					.css({
						top: function(){ 
							var nav = $('#gnf_dept_tree_nav&gt;ul, #deptNav'); /* Apparently either of these might be valid */ 
							return nav.length &gt; 0? (nav.offset().top + nav.height() + 20) : '';
						},
						left: '5px',
						position: 'absolute'
					});
				_mainContent
					.removeClass('span20')
					.addClass('span24');
				oasPositionRight = false;
			} else if (!oasPositionRight &amp;&amp; winWidth &gt; 1200) {
				_oasContainer
					.insertAfter(_mainContent)
					.css({
						'top': '',
						'left': '',
						'position': ''
					});
				_mainContent
					.removeClass('span24')
					.addClass('span20');
				oasPositionRight = true;
			}
		}
	if ($('#hdrv2').length) {
		_mainContent = $('.span20');
		_oasContainer = _mainContent.next() /* Mark OAS container for special CSS handling and shift position in the DOM */
					.attr('id','oas-container')
					.find('script').remove().end()
					.css('display', 'block');
		oasLegacySpacing();
	    setTimeout(function() {/* This was done via a deptNav complete() callback, but it no longer works */
	        oasLegacySpacing();
	    }, 450);
	    window.onresize = oasLegacySpacing;
	}
})
  </script>
  <script type="text/javascript">
   //Start BrightTag implementation - the regular bt site ID (shc:bt.site) is in high level page property 
//{'10151':'IctsMUI', '10151_QA':'QqDbVSM', '10153':'PCNPFl9','10153_QA':'for2rjl','10165':'PCNPFl9','10153_kiosk':'QDsdc7e','10151_kiosk':'fvqvh1D','10155':'BciA6ZX','10154':'mrIBbYB'}
window.btSiteMap = {'10153_kiosk':'QDsdc7e','10151_kiosk':'fvqvh1D'}; 
	window.bt = {"levelIds":"",
	"levels":"",
	"verticalId":"",
	"verticalName":"",
	"categoryID":"",
	"categoryName":"",
	"subCategoryID":"",
	"subCategoryName":"",
	"itemNumber":"",
	"beanType":"",
	"itemPrice":"N/A",
	"itemDiscount":"N/A",
	"productDescription":"",
	"oasSitePage":"sears.com/index/homepage"};
	(function() {
		var catArray = shc.catArray;
		var catIdArray =  shc.catIdArray;
		if (catArray.length &gt; 0) {
			var i = 0, l = Math.min(3, catArray.length);
			for (i = 0; i &lt; l; i++) {
				switch (i) {
					case 0:
						bt.verticalName = catArray[i];
						bt.levels = bt.verticalName;
						bt.verticalId = catIdArray[i];
						bt.levelIds = bt.verticalId;
						break;
					case 1:
						bt.categoryName = catArray[i];
						bt.levels += '_'+bt.categoryName;
						bt.categoryID = catIdArray[i];
						if(bt.categoryID !== ""){
						bt.levelIds += '_'+bt.categoryID;
						}
						break;
					case 2:
						bt.subCategoryName = catArray[i];
						bt.levels += '_'+bt.subCategoryName;
						bt.subCategoryID = catIdArray[i];
						if(bt.subCategoryID !== ""){
						bt.levelIds += '_'+bt.subCategoryID;
						}
				}
			}
		}
	})();
  </script>
